					A Life for the Tsar (Glinka, Mikhail)				</h1>

<table>
<table>

<tr>

</th>
<td>4 acts and Epilogue
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1836
</td></tr>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">A Life for the Tsar
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">Ivan Susanin
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Glinka,_Mikhail" title="Category:Glinka, Mikhail">Glinka, Mikhail</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IMG 23
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>4 acts and Epilogue
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1836
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Perf<span class="mh555">ormance</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1836-12-09 (27 November OS) in St. Petersburg, Bolshoi Kamenny Theatre <div class="expandline" style="background-color:#E8E8E8;margin-left:0;margin-top:0;padding:0">
<dl><dd>Osip Petrov (Ivan Susanin)<br />Mariya Stepanova (Antonida)<br />Anna Petrova-Vorobyova (Vanya)<br />Lev Leonov (Bogdan Sobinin)<br />Sergey Baykov (Polish commander)<br />I. Makarov (Polish courier)<br />Aleksey Yefremov (Russian commander)<br />Catterino Cavos (conductor) </div>
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1857, 1881 - St. Petersburg: F.T. Stellovsky <div class="expandline" style="background-color:#E8E8E8;margin-left:0;margin-top:0;padding:0">
<dl><dd><i>Vocal score</i> (1857)<br /><i>Full score</i> (1881) </div>
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Librettist
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Kukolnik,_Nestor" title="Category:Kukolnik, Nestor">Nestor Kukolnik</a>, <a href="/wiki/Category:Rosen,_Egor" title="Category:Rosen, Egor">Egor Rosen</a>, <a href="/wiki/Category:Sollogub,_Vladimir" title="Category:Sollogub, Vladimir">Vladimir Sollogub</a> and <a href="/wiki/Category:Zhukovsky,_Vasily" title="Category:Zhukovsky, Vasily">Vasily Zhukovsky</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Language
</th>
<td>Russian
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Composer Time Period</span><span class="ms555">Comp. Period</span>
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Romantic" title="Category:Romantic">Romantic</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Piece Style
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Romantic_style" title="Category:Romantic style">Romantic</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td>voices, chorus, orchestra <div class="expandline" style="background-color:#E8E8E8;margin-left:0;margin-top:0;padding:0">
<dl><dd><i>Cast</i>
<dl><dd>Ivan Susanin, a peasant of the village of Domnino (bass)<br />Antonida, his daughter (soprano)<br />Vanya, Susanin's adopted son (alto)<br />Bogdan Sobinin, a militiaman, Antonida's fiance (tenor)<br />Commander of the Polish Detachment (bass)<br />A Polish courier (tenor)<br />Commander of the Russian Detachment (bass)
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd><i>Mixed Chorus</i> 
<dl><dd>Peasant men and women, militiamen, Polish nobles and ladies, knights
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd><i>Orchestra</i>
<dl><dd>2 flutes, 2 oboes (2nd also English horn), 2 clarinets (B<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>/A), 2 bassoons<br />4 horns, 2 trumpets, 3 trombones, ophicleide<br /> timpani, bells, harp, strings
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd><i>Offstage instruments</i>
<dl><dd>2 wind bands, clarinet in A, trumpet, drum, bells </div>
</dd></dl>
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>External Links
</th>
<td><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/A_Life_for_the_Tsar" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:A Life for the Tsar">Wikipedia article</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Extra Information
</th>
<td>After the 1917 Russian Revolution a new libretto was prepared by <a href="/wiki/Category:Gorodetsky,_Sergey" title="Category:Gorodetsky, Sergey">Sergey Gorodetsky</a> (1884-1967), in which the name of the Tsar was replaced throughout. This Soviet version of the opera was renamed <i>Ivan Susanin</i> (which had in fact been Glinka's original working title for the opera, before it was premiered as <i>A Life for the Tsar</i>)
</td></tr></table>
</div>
